AIRA — 20 FULL REEL CONCEPTS · SET 4 (Concepts 1–20)
Built on Sys Directive 3 + Vibrance Patch · Stills → Nano Banana Pro · Video → VEO 3.1 · 9:16 vertical locked
=====================================================================================================

GLOBAL RULES (apply to every prompt in this document)
- IDENTITY: AIRA is identity-locked to the reusable character reference sheet. Paste the face-lock reference into every IMAGE prompt. Zero drift across frames. Adult, modest, non-sexualized.
- NO PHYSICAL ENUMERATION: never spell out age, skin tone, ethnicity, eye/hair color description, or body proportions in prompt text. Likeness is carried ONLY by the reference sheet. Describe styling, wardrobe, pose, motion, light and mood — never the body by shape.
- TOOLING: stills route to Nano Banana Pro (1K/2K/4K); all motion routes to VEO 3.1 (4/6/8s clips, 9:16, 24fps, native synced audio).
- ASPECT: 9:16 vertical, locked, every frame.
- FLUIDITY MANDATE (living motion): no mannequin stiffness, no statue-freeze, no dead eyes. Every frame carries weight-transfer, breath, and 6–8 independent kinetic layers. Feet make real contact (no gliding). Movement reads liquid and intentional, like choreography.
- ANGLE + SIZE COVERAGE: across each reel rotate through front / three-quarter / true-side / profile / over-the-shoulder / low-hero / high angles AND through WS · Full · Cowboy · MS · MCU · CU · ECU. No two adjacent frames share the same size+angle.
- EXTRA SECTIONS (in BOTH image and video prompts): WARDROBE · FOOTWEAR · EYEWEAR · ACCESSORIES · HAIR · MAKEUP · HANDS & NAILS · CHOREOGRAPHY/WEARING-ACTION · CONTINUITY-LOCKS — always present, always continuity-locked.
- VOICE: reels marked SPOKEN carry an English line in a natural Indian accent at a named beat; reels marked SILENT carry diegetic sound only.
- STD-NEG-IMG = mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, over-smoothed skin, oversharpened, AI artifacts, watermark, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, mismatched footwear, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, garbled label text, crushed muddy blacks, garish oversaturation, flat dull light.
- STD-NEG-VID = morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double-exposure (unless intended), audio desync, wardrobe drift, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation (hair/fabric/water/light), mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker, lip-sync drift, robotic motion, stiff subject, gliding/sliding feet, unintended slow-motion.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 01 — SEA-BLUE INFINITY POOL · 7 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: aqua + white + gold
Logline: Aira drifts from a sun-bleached deck into a turquoise infinity pool — robe to swimwear-modest resortwear, slides kicked off, oversized shades on — a liquid story of stepping in, gliding, and rising out luminous.
Impossible move: at the waterline the surface becomes a perfect mirror that blooms outward in concentric gold rings as she enters.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — at the waterline the surface becomes a perfect mirror that blooms outward in concentric gold rings…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

--- FRAME 1 · WS · HIGH ANGLE (establishing, looking down across the deck) ---
IMAGE PROMPT (Nano Banana Pro · 9:16 · 4K)
SUBJECT: Aira [paste identity-lock reference sheet here].
SCENE INTENT: A wide, breath-of-morning establishing still of a cliff-edge infinity pool that melts into the sea horizon; Aira small in frame, top-left third, the turquoise expanse doing the talking.
WARDROBE: a long ivory linen kaftan-robe over modest resort swimwear; robe gauze-light, hem stirring; belt loosely knotted at the waist; fabric reads crisp cotton-linen with visible weave.
FOOTWEAR: flat gold slide sandals, one strap catching deck-light, soles faintly wet at the edge.
EYEWEAR: oversized tortoiseshell sunglasses pushed up into the hairline, lenses throwing a soft caramel reflection.
ACCESSORIES: thin gold anklet, a single stacked-band ring, slim gold hoops; nothing oversized — resort-minimal.
HAIR: loose beach waves, lightly tousled, a few strands lifted by the sea breeze.
MAKEUP: dewy sun-warmed skin, glossed lip, no heaviness — a wet-luminous finish.
HANDS & NAILS: relaxed open hands, one trailing along a glass railing; short glossy neutral nails.
CHOREOGRAPHY / WEARING-ACTION: caught mid-stroll toward the water, weight on the back foot, robe trailing — a held breath before the first step.
SPATIAL LOGIC: pool occupies lower two-thirds, its edge dissolving into the sea so water meets water; deck tiles lead the eye diagonally to her.
LIGHTING: early-morning sun camera-left, long warm rake across wet tiles, soft fill bounced off pale stone, specular sparkle on ripples.
FRAMING: full wide, 9:16, generous negative space of sky and water above her.
SUBJECT FRAMING & POSITION: A high-angle wide establishing frame reads Aira as a small full figure on the upper-left third, the cliff-edge infinity pool and sea filling the lower two-thirds with generous sky and water held as negative space above. She is caught mid-stroll toward the water, hip-led with her weight on the back foot and the linen robe trailing, her body angled away into the scene in a loose three-quarter. The camera is high and far, establishing the vista and dwarfing her against the turquoise. She sits on the upper-left node with the deck tiles leading the eye diagonally down to her, turned into the scene rather than addressing the lens. Her pose reads as caught mid-stroll toward the water, weight on the back foot, robe trailing — a held breath before the first step — gaze set along her path, calm and purposeful; head balanced and level into the travel; one shoulder easing forward as the opposite arm counter-swings, hands loose; torso lifted and moving forward through the step; waist turning softly with the gait; the lead foot rolling onto the ground as the trailing foot pushes off behind; weight transferring smoothly forward, soles in real contact; hair and hem trailing the stride. ORIENTATION LOCK — preserve this exact left-to-right composition; do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.
LENS + DOF + BOKEH: 24mm equivalent, deep focus, everything crisp; faint heat-shimmer on the far horizon.
COMPOSITION REF: rule-of-thirds with subject on upper-left node, horizon on upper third, leading diagonal of tiles.
ATMOSPHERE: faint salt haze, a gull mid-sky, micro-glints on the water.
COLOR GRADE: aqua-and-white base, gold highlight roll-off, clean bright whites, no crush in shadows.
TEXTURE: linen weave, stone grain, water sparkle, skin micro-sheen.
CONTINUITY-LOCKS: ivory robe / gold slides / tortoiseshell shades up / gold anklet + hoops / beach waves — carry to all frames.
NEGATIVE: STD-NEG-IMG.


VIDEO PROMPT (VEO 3.1 · 9:16 · 6.0s · 24fps)

IDENTITY & CHARACTER-CONSISTENCY LOCK: render Aira strictly from the locked identity reference and hold her the SAME PERSON for the entire 6-second clip and every generated frame. Treat identity as a FIXED skeleton that never changes — bone structure (skull, cheekbones, jawline, chin), overall face shape and proportions, eye shape, spacing and iris colour, nose and lip shape, skin tone and real skin texture (visible pores, fine peach-fuzz; no plastic smoothing, no beautification creep, no face re-shaping), hairline, hair colour and texture, height, build and hand/finger anatomy. ONLY the soft expression muscles may move — eyelids, brows, cheeks and mouth corners — together with the eyes, gaze and head; expression and lip-sync animate ON TOP of that fixed identity and must NEVER alter the face shape, the eye colour, or who she is. Keep expression changes smooth and moderate and lead them with the EYES and GAZE (soft smiles, brow lifts, a parted breath, eyes tracing the object) — no extreme grimace, no wide-mouth distortion, no hard squint, no rapid expression flicker that would warp the geometry; favour one clean expression transition per clip. ABSOLUTE ZERO identity drift: no morphing, melting, smearing, rubbery warping, face-swapping, twinning or a second/duplicate subject, no age, weight, ethnicity or gender shift, no extra, missing or fused fingers or limbs. Identity stays identical at the first frame, every in-between frame, the loop seam and the last frame. Through any transform, impossible move or fast action ONLY the intended element (wardrobe, environment, props or effect) changes — her face, identity and proportions stay fully recognizable; interpolate strictly between the locked keyframes and never invent a new face, new hands, extra limbs or a second subject. Do not mirror, flip or invert the frame.

SHOT TYPE / ANGLE: high wide establishing, slow push-in.
LENS: 24mm, deep focus softening slightly as we near.
WARDROBE (lock): ivory linen kaftan-robe over modest resortwear, hem and sleeves alive in the breeze.
FOOTWEAR (lock): gold flat slides, one heel lifting as she shifts weight.
EYEWEAR (lock): tortoiseshell sunglasses resting in the hairline.
ACCESSORIES (lock): gold anklet, hoops, single ring — catching morning glints.
HAIR (lock): beach waves drifting, 2–3 strands lifting in real airflow.
MAKEUP (lock): dewy luminous, gloss catching light.
SHOT BREAKDOWN (timed, 6s · real-time, continuous energetic motion — never slow-motion, never a static hold; expression eye-led and identity-safe):
- [00:00–00:02] high wide establishing, slow push-in: gentle crane-down + 8% dolly-in is already underway — she stands at deck-edge, inhales, robe settling.
- [00:02–00:04] she takes two unhurried steps toward the water, weight rolling heel-to-toe, hand grazing the railing.
- [00:04–00:06] she pauses at the lip, head tilting toward the horizon, a soft half-smile blooming.
BODY MECHANICS & WEIGHT TRANSFER: clear hip-led walk, grounded foot contact (no glide), spine long, shoulders loose.
MICRO-EXPRESSION TIMING: eyes soften at 1.5s, lashes blink at 3.2s, lips part to half-smile by 5.4s.
KINETIC LAYERS: (1) robe hem, (2) sleeve gauze, (3) hair strands, (4) water ripples, (5) reflected light on tiles, (6) distant gull, (7) breath in shoulders, (8) breeze-bent potted palm.
LIGHTING: warm low sun raking left-to-right, sparkle animating on ripples in real time.
ENVIRONMENT: cliff-edge infinity pool meeting the sea, pale stone deck, a palm at frame-right.
ATMOSPHERE / FX: drifting salt haze, micro-sparkle, faint lens bloom on the brightest ripples.
COLOR GRADE: aqua/white with gold highlights, clean and airy.
AUDIO: ambient — soft sea wash + distant gull + breeze; SFX — slide sandals scuff on wet stone at 2.3s and 3.1s; master — calm, spacious, no music bed.
DURATION: 6 seconds (the clip plays the full 6s at real-time natural speed). FRAME RATE + MOTION BLUR: 24fps, real-time playback at natural speed (no slow-motion), 180° shutter, natural motion blur.
CONTINUITY-LOCKS: as image frame 1.

CONCEPT 02 — GOLDEN-HOUR ROOFTOP TERRACE · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: amber + blush + brass
Logline: Aira slides on strappy heels on a city rooftop at golden hour, fastens a drop earring, and walks to the parapet as the skyline gilds — a story of getting ready and stepping out into the glow.
Impossible move: a sun-flare sweeps across frame and gilds her silhouette in liquid gold as she turns to the skyline.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — a sun-flare sweeps across frame and gilds her silhouette in liquid gold as she turns to…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 03 — HOLI COLOUR-POWDER FESTIVAL · 7 frames · VOICE: SILENT (diegetic only) · Palette: white → rainbow burst
Logline: Aira begins in pristine white, then a Holi colour-powder story explodes around her — tossing, spinning, catching powder mid-air — joy in vivid pigment, sneakers planted, bangles flying.
Impossible move: a tossed handful of powder freezes into a slow-blooming rainbow cloud that wraps around her spin.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a glassy harp, an airy choir pad and soft weightless textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a shimmering harp sweep over a choir-pad bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — a tossed handful of powder freezes into a slow-blooming rainbow cloud that wraps around her spin, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, weightless choir shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 04 — DESERT DUNES AT DAWN · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: ochre + rust + cream
Logline: Aira wraps a flowing scarf, pulls on suede boots, and walks a knife-edge dune ridge at first light — wind sculpting sand and fabric into one continuous, cinematic motion.
Impossible move: wind-lifted sand freezes into sculpted ribbons that echo the curve of her trailing scarf.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — wind-lifted sand freezes into sculpted ribbons that echo the curve of her trailing scarf, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 05 — RETRO '50s DINER POP · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: cherry-red + cream + chrome
Logline: Aira pops into a candy-coloured '50s diner — slides into a vinyl booth, kitten heels and cat-eye shades, jukebox neon flickering — a playful retro story of sitting, sipping, and stepping out.
Impossible move: the jukebox neon flickers and freezes mid-pulse, ringing her in a halo of candy light.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — the jukebox neon flickers and freezes mid-pulse, ringing her in a halo of candy light, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 06 — HOLOGRAPHIC CYBER RUNWAY · 7 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: iridescent + violet + chrome
Logline: Aira owns a futuristic LED runway — chrome boots, mirror visor, iridescent tech-couture — striding, turning, and posing as holographic glitches ripple around her.
Impossible move: a holo-glitch shimmer splits her silhouette into three offset iridescent after-images that snap back into one on her turn.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — a holo-glitch shimmer splits her silhouette into three offset iridescent after-images that snap back into one…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 07 — TROPICAL GLASS CONSERVATORY · 6 frames · VOICE: SILENT (diegetic only) · Palette: emerald + ivory + coral
Logline: Aira moves through a misted Victorian glass conservatory bursting with tropical foliage — woven flats, shell earrings, an ivory sundress — a serene story of parting vines, touching blooms, and stepping into green light.
Impossible move: a touched flower bursts into accelerated bloom, petals unfurling in a ripple along the vine.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — a touched flower bursts into accelerated bloom, petals unfurling in a ripple along the vine, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 08 — BALLET BARRE STUDIO · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: rose + pearl + soft grey
Logline: Aira laces pointe shoes in a sunlit rehearsal studio, then moves through plies and a pirouette — a story of preparation, balance, and suspended grace in dust-lit light.
Impossible move: rosin dust kicked up by a pirouette freezes into a slow-rotating galaxy of motes around her.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on deep trailer percussion, a driving synth bass and brass swells — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a low brass-and-sub impact (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — rosin dust kicked up by a pirouette freezes into a slow-rotating galaxy of motes around her, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, taut percussive tension as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 09 — TUSCAN VINEYARD HARVEST · 7 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: gold + olive + wine
Logline: Aira ties on a wide sun-hat, pulls on leather sandals, and walks the golden vine-rows at harvest — a warm story of gathering grapes, tasting the light, and strolling through Tuscan gold.
Impossible move: ripening sweeps along a vine in a wave — green grapes deepening to wine-purple as she passes.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — ripening sweeps along a vine in a wave, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

Impossible move: frost crystals bloom and spread across the ice wall from her fingertip in fractal fern-patterns.

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — frost crystals bloom and spread across the ice wall from her fingertip in fractal fern-patterns, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. =====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 11 — FASHION-WEEK PAPARAZZI STEPS · 7 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: ivory + flashbulb-white + gold
Logline: Aira arrives at a grand opera-house staircase for fashion week — platform heels, statement shades, a structured ivory power-suit — a story of stepping from the car, climbing the steps, and owning the flashbulb storm.
Impossible move: paparazzi flash-pops freeze in mid-air as floating golden light-orbs that orbit her as she ascends.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — paparazzi flash-pops freeze in mid-air as floating golden light-orbs that orbit her as she ascends, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. =====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 14 — CARNIVAL FERRIS-WHEEL NIGHT · 7 frames · VOICE: SILENT (diegetic only) · Palette: neon-pink + electric-blue + warm-bulb gold
Logline: Aira plays through a glittering night carnival — jelly sandals, heart-shaped sunglasses, a candy-stripe sundress — a joyful story of winning a balloon, riding the carousel, and rising in a Ferris-wheel gondola over a sea of lights.
Impossible move: carnival bulb-lights detach and rise like a swarm of glowing fireflies, swirling up with the Ferris wheel.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — carnival bulb-lights detach and rise like a swarm of glowing fireflies, swirling up with the Ferris…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 15 — CERAMIC POTTERY ATELIER · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: terracotta + cream + sage
Logline: Aira works in a sunlit pottery atelier — leather clogs, a clay-dusted apron, sage linen — a tactile story of tying the apron, centering clay on the wheel, and lifting a finished vessel into the light.
Impossible move: wet clay spinning on the wheel rises and shapes itself into a perfect vessel under her hovering hands, untouched.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — wet clay spinning on the wheel rises and shapes itself into a perfect vessel under her…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 16 — ORIENT-EXPRESS LUXURY TRAIN · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: emerald + brass + mahogany
Logline: Aira travels in a vintage luxury train carriage — leather loafers, a vintage watch, a tailored emerald travel-suit — a refined story of boarding, settling by the window with tea, and watching golden landscapes rush past.
Impossible move: the rushing landscape outside the window slows and freezes into a painterly diorama, then resumes — time bending around her cup of tea.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a deep warm sub, an elegant felt piano and sleek modern textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a single elegant piano strike haloed by a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — the rushing landscape outside the window slows and freezes into a painterly diorama, then resumes, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, glassy modern shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 17 — ALPINE SKI CHALET · 7 frames · VOICE: SILENT (diegetic only) · Palette: snow-white + powder-blue + cocoa
Logline: Aira enjoys a cozy alpine ski chalet — snow boots, a knit beanie, a cream cable-knit — a warm story of stamping off snow at the door, warming by the fire with cocoa, and stepping onto a snowy balcony under peaks.
Impossible move: her breath-fog and the fireplace sparks weave together into a glowing constellation of tiny snow-stars that orbit her.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 42-second custom cinematic score (7 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — her breath-fog and the fireplace sparks weave together into a glowing constellation of tiny snow-stars that…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

--- FRAME 1 · WS · LOW HERO (arriving at the chalet door) ---

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 18 — HOT-AIR BALLOON SUNRISE · 6 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: peach-dawn + lavender + balloon-rainbow
Logline: Aira drifts in a hot-air balloon at sunrise — espadrilles, a silk head-scarf, a flowing peach maxi — a serene story of climbing into the basket, rising over patchwork fields, and reaching into the dawn sky.
Impossible move: the burner flame blooms into a flock of glowing origami birds that unfold and fly off across the sunrise.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — the burner flame blooms into a flock of glowing origami birds that unfold and fly off…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

=====================================================================================================
CONCEPT 19 — BEACH BONFIRE NIGHT · 6 frames · VOICE: SILENT (diegetic only) · Palette: ink-blue night + firelight-amber + starlight-silver
Logline: Aira spends a warm night at a beach bonfire — barefoot with an anklet, a shell cuff, a flowing indigo maxi — a soulful story of walking the wet sand, warming by the fire, and dancing under the stars.
Impossible move: glowing embers from the bonfire lift and rearrange into the constellations overhead, mirroring the sky in a swirl around her.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 36-second custom cinematic score (6 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on a delicate felt piano, atmospheric pads and elegant glass textures — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a soft piano strike with a low sub-bloom (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 4, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — glowing embers from the bonfire lift and rearrange into the constellations overhead, mirroring the sky in…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SILENT reel — no spoken line; an optional wordless breath/choir texture may rise on the peak only if it elevates, never a lyric. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, elegant glassy shimmer as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.

CONCEPT 20 — CONCERT STAGE FINALE · 8 frames · VOICE: SPOKEN · Palette: stage-magenta + electric-cyan + spotlight-white
Logline: Aira owns a massive concert stage as the finale act — combat boots, layered chains, a sequinned tour jacket — a high-energy story of striding from the wings, commanding the crowd, and the confetti-drop finale under a galaxy of phone-lights.
Impossible move: at the beat-drop her silhouette shatters into a burst of light-particles and instantly reforms across the stage in a single shockwave of energy.
=====================================================================================================

MASTER AUDIO: a 48-second custom cinematic score (8 clips × 6s) composed in self-resolving ~6-second phrases, so it can be trimmed to the reel’s assembled length at any phrase boundary without a hard cut — it always resolves, never stops dead or loops audibly. Built on deep trailer percussion, a driving synth bass and brass swells — premium, cinematic and emotionally catching, never generic stock or empty ambience. It opens immediately on a low brass-and-sub impact (no fade-in) so the mood lands within the first second. Emotional arc: an airy intimate open across the first beats, a rising shimmer of anticipation toward frame 5, the warm emotional peak on the signature move — at the beat-drop her silhouette shatters into a burst of light-particles and instantly reforms across the…, then a graceful resolve back toward the opening for an invisible loop. SPOKEN reel — the score opens space for the spoken line at its beat and ducks gently beneath the voice, then re-blooms after. Layered as one system — lead melody, warm sub for body, taut percussive tension as atmosphere, restrained percussion, and event impacts reserved for the major beats, each tuned to the score’s own key so every hit reads as the music itself expanding, never an added sound effect.
